  <script type="text/javascript">
    (function() {
        var contextPath = '/jira';
        var eventBuffer = [];

        function printDeprecatedMsg() {
            if (console && console.warn) {
                console.warn('DEPRECATED JS - contextPath global variable has been deprecated since 7.4.0. Use `wrm/context-path` module instead.');
            }
        }

        function sendEvent(analytics, postfix) {
            analytics.send({
                name: 'js.globals.contextPath.' + postfix
            });
        }

        function sendDeprecatedEvent(postfix) {
            try {
                var analytics = require('jira/analytics');
                if (eventBuffer.length) {
                    eventBuffer.forEach(function(value) {
                        sendEvent(analytics, value);
                    });
                    eventBuffer = [];
                }

                if (postfix) {
                    sendEvent(analytics, postfix);
                }
            } catch(ex) {
                eventBuffer.push(postfix);
                setTimeout(sendDeprecatedEvent, 1000);
            }
        }

        Object.defineProperty(window, 'contextPath', {
            get: function() {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('get');
                return contextPath;
            },
            set: function(value) {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('set');
                contextPath = value;
            }
        });
    })();

</script>

                  </div> </li> 
                 <li class="item new"> 
                  <div class="wrap"> 
                   <strong class="name">Priority:</strong> 
                   <span id="priority-val" class="value"> <img alt="" height="16" src="/jira/images/icons/priorities/major.svg" title="Major - Major loss of function." width="16"> Major </span>

                  <div class="wrap">

              <div id="descriptionmodule" class="module toggle-wrap">
               <div id="descriptionmodule_heading" class="mod-header">
                <ul class="ops"></ul>
                <h2 class="toggle-title">Description</h2>
               </div>
               <div class="mod-content">
                <div id="description-val" class="field-ignore-highlight"> 
                 <div class="user-content-block"> 
                  <p>We have a bunch of redundant methods in our matrix interface. These include things that return views of parts of the matrix:</p> 
                  <div class="code panel" style="border-width: 1px;">
                   <div class="codeContent panelContent"> 
                    <pre class="code-java">  Matrix viewPart(<span class="code-object">int</span>[] offset, <span class="code-object">int</span>[] size);
  Matrix viewPart(<span class="code-object">int</span> rowOffset, <span class="code-object">int</span> rowsRequested, <span class="code-object">int</span> columnOffset, <span class="code-object">int</span> columnsRequested);
  Vector viewRow(<span class="code-object">int</span> row);
  Vector viewColumn(<span class="code-object">int</span> column);
</pre> 
                   </div>
                  </div> 
                  <p>and things that do the same but call refer to getting stuff</p> 
                  <div class="code panel" style="border-width: 1px;">
                   <div class="codeContent panelContent"> 
                    <pre class="code-java">  Vector getColumn(<span class="code-object">int</span> column);
  Vector getRow(<span class="code-object">int</span> row);
  <span class="code-object">double</span> getQuick(<span class="code-object">int</span> row, <span class="code-object">int</span> column);
  <span class="code-object">int</span>[] getNumNondefaultElements();
  Map&lt;<span class="code-object">String</span>, <span class="code-object">Integer</span>&gt; getColumnLabelBindings();
  Map&lt;<span class="code-object">String</span>, <span class="code-object">Integer</span>&gt; getRowLabelBindings();
  <span class="code-object">double</span> get(<span class="code-object">String</span> rowLabel, <span class="code-object">String</span> columnLabel);
</pre> 
                   </div>
                  </div> 
                  <p>To my mind, get implies a get-by-value whereas view implies get-by-reference. As such, I would suggest that getColumn and getRow should disappear. On the other hand, getQuick and get are both correctly named. </p> 
                  <p>This raises the question of what getNumNondefaultElements really does. I certainly can't tell just from the signature. Is it too confusing to keep?</p> 
                  <p>Additionally, what do people think that getColumnLabelBindings and getRowLabelBindings return? A mutable map? Or an immutable one?</p> 
                  <p>Under the covers, viewRow and viewColumn (and the upcoming viewDiagonal) have default implementations that use MatrixVectorView, but AbstractMatrix doesn't have an implementation for getRow and getColumn. </p> 
                  <p>In sum, I suggest that:</p> 
                  <ul class="alternate" type="square"> 
                   <li>getRow and getColumn go away</li> 
                  </ul> 
                  <ul class="alternate" type="square"> 
                   <li>the fancy fast implementations fo getRow and getColumn that exist be migrated to be over-rides of viewRow and viewColumn</li> 
                  </ul> 
                  <ul class="alternate" type="square"> 
                   <li>there be a constructor for AbstractMatrix that sets the internal size things correctly.</li> 
                  </ul> 
                  <ul class="alternate" type="square"> 
                   <li>that the internal cardinality array in AbstractMatrix goes away to be replaced by two integers.</li> 
                  </ul> 
                  <ul class="alternate" type="square"> 
                   <li>viewDiagonal() and viewDiagonal(length) and viewDiagonal(row, column) and viewDiagonal(int row, column, length) be added.</li> 
                  </ul> 
                  <p>I will produce a patch shortly.</p> 
                 </div> 
                </div> 
               </div>
              </div>

So far, this isn\'t a big deal although I do have a triangular solver in my CholeskyDecomposition.  If we see some more uses, it might be worth pulling out as a separate class. \\n\\n I don\'t see that a SymmetricMatrix is an important thing yet.  Yes, there are important mathematical properties there, but these aren\'t necessarily something worth reflecting in the type structure.  Good use cases would change my mind. \\n\\n \\n Example: DiagonalMatrix.invert() is a valid method, because it either blows up if there is a 0 value, or returns 1\\/values.  \\n I prefer solve methods rather than invert methods.  It is already much too hard to cure people of trying to invert matrices. As the name suggests viewDiagonal is a view method so it would be bad to make it read-only.  It does make certain operations like computing the determinant very simple: \\n  \\n   determinant =  new  CholeskyDecomposition(matrix).viewDiagonal().aggregate(Functions.TIMES)\\n \\n  \\n or setting the diagonal of a matrix to all zeros: \\n  \\n  \\n   m.viewDiagonal().assign(0)\\n \\n  \\n\\n The diagonal matrix is handy when reconstructing SVD\'s.  You get this: \\n\\n  \\n    u.times( new  DiagonalMatrix(singularValues)).times(v.transpose())\\n \\n  \\n\\n Since the DiagonalMatrix is marked as sparse, efficiency is good. There\'s an operation that gives a separate, identical copy with all the same values. There\'s also an operation that gives a separate, identical copy with no data or values.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThe first should certainly be called clone(), since that\'s what it is, in Java.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eLance, is your objection that we simply should not have the first operation? or that you don\'t want to use clone() per se for some reason?\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\nI don\'t see that either of these two has an easier time deciding what class to return, or that one or the other must or must not be implemented in subclasses. These are like any other OO method.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eI can imagine both are useful, and so would support keeping both. If someone has a good argument that one or the other really isn\'t used, that\'s good too. And certainly if we\'re finding they\'re implemented incorrectly, and I did find several instances of that in the past, we should fix it.\u003c\\/p\u003e \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap concise actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Expand comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-collapsed\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eShow\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details flooded\\\"\u003e\\n                        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"srowen\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_13088634_concise\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=srowen\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"srowen\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Sean Owen\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13088634_concise subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'22\\/Aug\\/11 12:00\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2011-08-22T12:00:49+0000\'\u003e22\\/Aug\\/11 12:00\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e                    On clone() vs like(): there are two logical operations we might want to support here. There\'s an operation that gives a separate, identical copy with all the same values. There\'s also an operation that gives a separate, identical copy with no data or values. \\n\\n The first should certainly be called clone(), since that\'s what it is, in Java. \\n\\n Lance, is your objection that we simply should not have the first operation? or that you don\'t want to use clone() per se for some reason? \\nI don\'t see that either of these two has an easier time deciding what class to return, or that one or the other must or must not be implemented in subclasses. These are like any other OO method. \\n\\n I can imagine both are useful, and so would support keeping both. If someone has a good argument that one or the other really isn\'t used, that\'s good too. And certainly if we\'re finding they\'re implemented incorrectly, and I did find several instances of that in the past, we should fix it.              \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-body flooded\\\"\u003e\u003cp\u003eSean,\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eWe definitely need both operations.  The first can be expressed, however, as a.like().assign(a) so it isn\'t quite as necessary as it might seem.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThe problem with clone itself is that there are serious restrictions on how you have to do it based on Java requirements.  That makes it a royal pain some days of the week.  This may be easier after this JIRA gets resolved since the only information at AbstractMatrix level is the number of rows and columns and they are trivial to deal with.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eWe definitely also have some bugs in our test suite in that it is assumed that like() has to return the same type of object.  That isn\'t really true.  For instance, m.viewPart(0,3,2,5).like() should return the same thing that m.like() returns.  But viewPart probably returns some kind of view object so these aren\'t the same.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eI can deal with those issues another day.  \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eIf we can get eyes on this monster patch, I would like to commit it shortly.  The only big issues I know about are:\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003ea) getRow and getColumn is a more common name than viewRow and viewColumn.  Does everybody promise not to be confused by the loss of getRow?\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eb) what should the iterator of a matrix do?  Right now SparseColumnMatrix iterates over columns and everything else by rows. The first can be expressed, however, as a.like().assign(a) so it isn\'t quite as necessary as it might seem. \\n\\n The problem with clone itself is that there are serious restrictions on how you have to do it based on Java requirements.  That makes it a royal pain some days of the week.  This may be easier after this JIRA gets resolved since the only information at AbstractMatrix level is the number of rows and columns and they are trivial to deal with. \\n\\n We definitely also have some bugs in our test suite in that it is assumed that like() has to return the same type of object.  That isn\'t really true.  For instance, m.viewPart(0,3,2,5).like() should return the same thing that m.like() returns.  But viewPart probably returns some kind of view object so these aren\'t the same. \\n\\n I can deal with those issues another day.   \\n\\n If we can get eyes on this monster patch, I would like to commit it shortly.  The only big issues I know about are: \\n\\n a) getRow and getColumn is a more common name than viewRow and viewColumn.  Does everybody promise not to be confused by the loss of getRow? \\n\\n b) what should the iterator of a matrix do?  Right now SparseColumnMatrix iterates over columns and everything else by rows.  Unless there is some very clear way to tell what the iteration is doing, I would like to go on record as grumpy about that.              \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13090377_verbose subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'24\\/Aug\\/11 18:09\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2011-08-24T18:09:06+0000\'\u003e24\\/Aug\\/11 18:09\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e  \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-body flooded\\\"\u003e\u003cblockquote\u003e\\n\u003cp\u003eBut it does show that perhaps viewPart should be done outside of Matrix.\u003c\\/p\u003e\u003c\\/blockquote\u003e\\n\u003cp\u003eI think not.  Getting a view of a submatrix or row or column or diagonal is a fundamental operation in linear algebra. The method may delegate to a view class, but to the user, it should appear as a matrix operation.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eBesides, there are are kinds of matrices and vectors where the view \u003cb\u003eis\u003c\\/b\u003e the same type as the matrix.  For instance, for dense matrices this is often true because the dense matrix is a one-dimensional storage array combined with an offset plus row and column strides.  Any block-wise view of this keeps the same storage and has different offset and strides.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eOn the other hand, sparse matrices do better with a view structure.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eIn any caes, viewPart should be a method on the matrix.  It should return a matrix and preserve sparsity and maybe a few related properties, but not precise type.\u003c\\/p\u003e \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap concise actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Expand comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-collapsed\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eShow\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details flooded\\\"\u003e\\n                        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"tdunning\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_13090377_concise\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=tdunning\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"tdunning\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Ted Dunning\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13090377_concise subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'24\\/Aug\\/11 18:09\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2011-08-24T18:09:06+0000\'\u003e24\\/Aug\\/11 18:09\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e                    \\n But it does show that perhaps viewPart should be done outside of Matrix.  \\n I think not.  Getting a view of a submatrix or row or column or diagonal is a fundamental operation in linear algebra. The method may delegate to a view class, but to the user, it should appear as a matrix operation. \\n\\n Besides, there are are kinds of matrices and vectors where the view  is  the same type as the matrix.  For instance, for dense matrices this is often true because the dense matrix is a one-dimensional storage array combined with an offset plus row and column strides.  Any block-wise view of this keeps the same storage and has different offset and strides. \\n\\n On the other hand, sparse matrices do better with a view structure. \\n\\n In any caes, viewPart should be a method on the matrix.  It should return a matrix and preserve sparsity and maybe a few related properties, but not precise type.              \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n\u003c\\/div\u003e\\n                             \\n\\n\\n\u003cdiv id=\\\"comment-13095234\\\" class=\\\"issue-data-block activity-comment twixi-block  expanded\\\"\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap verbose actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Collapse comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-expanded\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eHide\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-links\\\"\u003e\\n                \u003ca href=\\\"\\/jira\\/browse\\/MAHOUT-790?focusedCommentId=13095234&page=com.atlassian.jira.plugin.system.issuetabpanels:comment-tabpanel#comment-13095234\\\"\\n                   title=\\\"Right click and copy link for a permanent link to this comment.\\\" class=\\\"activitymodule-link issue-comment-action\\\"\u003e\\n                    \u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-link\\\"\u003ePermalink\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n                                            \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details\\\"\u003e        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"tdunning\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_13095234_verbose\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=tdunning\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"tdunning\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Ted Dunning\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - Since the pivoted matrix is just a view, this should be easy to make happen. It probably doesn\'t happen correctly now.  \\n\\n Matrix row&amp;column labels are string-&gt;index maps. If you write code that knows it has a permuted matrix, it can pull the labels and the permutation lists and do the indirection. If it does not know it has a permuted matrix, it will get non-tracking outputs. \\n             \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n\u003c\\/div\u003e\\n                             \\n\\n\\n\u003cdiv id=\\\"comment-13103479\\\" class=\\\"issue-data-block activity-comment twixi-block  expanded\\\"\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap verbose actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Collapse comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-expanded\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eHide\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-links\\\"\u003e\\n                \u003ca href=\\\"\\/jira\\/browse\\/MAHOUT-790?focusedCommentId=13103479&page=com.atlassian.jira.plugin.system.issuetabpanels:comment-tabpanel#comment-13103479\\\"\\n                   title=\\\"Right click and copy link for a permanent link to this comment.\\\" class=\\\"activitymodule-link issue-comment-action\\\"\u003e\\n                    \u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-link\\\"\u003ePermalink\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n                                            \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details\\\"\u003e        \\n    \\n    \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"srowen\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_13103479_verbose\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=srowen\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"srowen\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Sean Owen\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  -
